module RT-VALUE-SYNTAX [digest(w0dXuaPkFo2Hp1VoTlJz6fgkhg3WKBC8k6EqJ0zY2B8=), org.kframework.attributes.Location(Location(11,1,160,10)), org.kframework.attributes.Source(Source(/home/daniel/.cache/kdist-a315c6b/mir-semantics/source/mir-semantics/rt/value.md))]
  imports TYPES
  imports MONO
  imports LIB
  imports BODY
  syntax Value ::= "valueOf" "(" TypedValue ")" [function, total]
  syntax Value ::= "Union" "(" FieldIdx "," Value ")" [symbol(Value::Union)]
  syntax Value ::= "StringVal" "(" String ")" [symbol(Value::StringVal)]
  syntax Value ::= "Reference" "(" Int "," Place "," Mutability "," Metadata ")" [symbol(Value::Reference)]
  syntax Value ::= "Range" "(" List ")" [symbol(Value::Range)]
  syntax Value ::= "PtrLocal" "(" Int "," Place "," Mutability "," Metadata ")" [symbol(Value::PtrLocal)]
  syntax Value ::= "Moved"
  syntax Value ::= "Integer" "(" Int "," Int "," Bool ")" [symbol(Value::Integer)]
